TARGET TRADING ACTIVITY (filtered)

## Field Guide
- Market: Polymarket up/down binary market. Pays $1 if correct, $0 if wrong.
- T+: Seconds into the window when trade was placed (T+11s = 11s after window opened)
- Outcome: Up or Down — which side of the binary bet (bot always BUYs)
- Price: Cost per share ($0.65 = 65c). Winning share pays $1
- Crypto$: Live Binance price at exact moment of trade
- Ref$: Crypto price at window start — the price-to-beat for Up vs Down
- Delta%: (Crypto$ - Ref$) / Ref$ — positive = Up winning, negative = Down winning
- Aligns?: YES = betting WITH the price move (directional), hedge = betting AGAINST (insurance)
- Bid: Best price someone will pay to buy this token on Polymarket at trade time
- Ask: Lowest price someone will sell this token for on Polymarket at trade time
- Spread: Ask minus Bid. Tight (0.01) = liquid market, easy entry/exit. Wide (0.05+) = thin book, bot pays premium for speed. Compare trade Price vs Bid/Ask to see if bot uses market orders (buys at ask) or limit orders (buys near bid)
- Result: WON = this outcome was the winner (pays $1/share). LOST = other side won ($0/share). Empty = not yet resolved

Assets: BTC, ETH, SOL, XRP, OTHER
